     1 import { serve } from 'https://deno.land/std@0.168.0/http/server.ts'
     2 
     3 const GITHUB_API_BASE = 'https://api.github.com'
     4 
     5 const corsHeaders = {
     6   'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
     7   'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type',
     8   'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'POST, OPTIONS',
     9 }
    10 
    11 function githubHeaders(token?: string) {
    12   const headers: Record<string, string> = {
    13     'Accept': 'application/vnd.github+json',
    14     'X-GitHub-Api-Version': '2022-11-28',
    15     'User-Agent': 'OpenAppStore/1.0',
    16   }
    17   if (token) {
    18     headers['Authorization'] = `Bearer ${token}`
    19   }
    20   return headers
    21 }
    22 
    23 serve(async (req) => {
    24   if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') {
    25     return new Response('ok', { headers: corsHeaders })
    26   }
    27 
    28   try {
    29     const { action, params, token } = await req.json()
    30     let url: string
    31     let method = 'GET'
    32 
    33     switch (action) {
    34       case 'search': {
    35         const q = params?.q || 'topic:android-app OR topic:ios-app OR topic:electron'
    36         const sort = params?.sort || 'stars'
    37         const order = params?.order || 'desc'
    38         const page = params?.page || 1
    39         const perPage = params?.per_page || 30
    40         url = `${GITHUB_API_BASE}/search/repositories?q=${encodeURIComponent(q)}&sort=${sort}&order=${order}&page=${page}&per_page=${perPage}`
    41         break
    42       }
    43       case 'repo': {
    44         const owner = params?.owner
    45         const repo = params?.repo
    46         if (!owner || !repo) throw new Error('Missing owner or repo')
    47         url = `${GITHUB_API_BASE}/repos/${owner}/${repo}`
    48         break
    49       }
    50       case 'releases': {
    51         const owner = params?.owner
    52         const repo = params?.repo
    53         const page = params?.page || 1
    54         if (!owner || !repo) throw new Error('Missing owner or repo')
    55         url = `${GITHUB_API_BASE}/repos/${owner}/${repo}/releases?page=${page}&per_page=20`
    56         break
    57       }
    58       case 'readme': {
    59         const owner = params?.owner
    60         const repo = params?.repo
    61         if (!owner || !repo) throw new Error('Missing owner or repo')
    62         url = `${GITHUB_API_BASE}/repos/${owner}/${repo}/readme`
    63         break
    64       }
    65       case 'contributors': {
    66         const owner = params?.owner
    67         const repo = params?.repo
    68         if (!owner || !repo) throw new Error('Missing owner or repo')
    69         url = `${GITHUB_API_BASE}/repos/${owner}/${repo}/contributors?per_page=10`
    70         break
    71       }
    72       case 'rate_limit': {
    73         url = `${GITHUB_API_BASE}/rate_limit`
    74         break
    75       }
    76       default:
    77         throw new Error(`Unknown action: ${action}`)
    78     }
    79 
    80     const response = await fetch(url, {
    81       method,
    82       headers: githubHeaders(token),
    83     })
    84 
    85     if (!response.ok) {
    86       const errorText = await response.text()
    87       return new Response(
    88         JSON.stringify({ error: `GitHub API error: ${response.status}`, details: errorText }),
    89         { status: response.status, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } }
    90       )
    91     }
    92 
    93     const data = await response.json()
    94 
    95     return new Response(JSON.stringify({ data, headers: Object.fromEntries(response.headers.entries()) }), {
    96       headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    97     })
    98   } catch (error) {
    99     return new Response(
   100       JSON.stringify({ error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error' }),
   101       { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } }
   102     )
   103   }

```
New String: ```
export function filterInstallAssets(assets: GitHubRelease['assets']) {
  // 明确的安装包扩展名（与 hasInstallerAsset 保持完全一致）
  const installerExts = [
    '.apk', '.xapk', '.aab',                              // Android
    '.ipa',                                                // iOS
    '.exe', '.msi', '.msix', '.msixbundle',                // Windows
    '.dmg', '.pkg',                                        // macOS
    '.deb', '.rpm', '.appimage', '.snap', '.flatpak',      // Linux
    '.zip', '.tar.gz', '.tar.bz2', '.tar.xz', '.7z', '.rar', // 安装包归档
  ]
  // 排除类：校验/签名/元数据/调试符号（与 hasInstallerAsset 保持完全一致）
  const excludeExts = [
    '.asc', '.sig', '.sha256', '.sha512', '.sha1', '.md5',
    '.txt', '.json', '.yaml', '.yml', '.xml',
    '.pdb', '.blockmap', '.nupkg', '.map', '.wasm',
    '.log', '.md', '.rst', '.pdf',
  ]

  return assets.filter((a) => {
    const lower = a.name.toLowerCase()
    // 1. 命中明确安装包扩展名 → 显示
    if (installerExts.some((ext) => lower.endsWith(ext))) return true
    // 2. 命中排除类 → 不显示
    if (excludeExts.some((ext) => lower.endsWith(ext))) return false
    // 3. 兜底：其他 >50KB 文件视为潜在安装包（与 hasInstallerAsset 一致）
    return a.size > 50 * 1024
  })
}
```

兜底），"快捷下载"区块改为查找第一个含真实安装包的版本进行展示。# Issue\n修复详情页安装包不显示的过滤逻辑不一致问题'}, thought='Lint 通过，全部修复完成。\n# Summary\n修复了详情页安装包不显示的问题，根本原因有两处：① `filterInstallAssets`（详情页展示）与 `hasInstallerAsset`（列表过滤）逻辑不一致——前者仅排除 6     41 export default function HomeTab() {
    42   const router = useRouter();

    44   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

    55   const loadData = useCallback(async (pageNum = 1, isRefresh = false, catKey = activeCategory, installerFilter = onlyInstaller) => {
    56     if (loadingRef.current && !isRefresh) return;
    57     loadingRef.current = true;
    58     try {
    59       setError('');
    60       if (isRefresh) setRefreshing(true);
    61       else if (pageNum === 1) setLoading(true);
    62 
    63       const query = buildQuery(catKey);
    64       const { items } = await searchRepos(query, { page: pageNum, per_page: 30, sort: 'stars' });
    65 
    66       let finalItems = items;
    67       if (installerFilter) {
    68         setFiltering(true);
    69         try {
    70           finalItems = await filterAppsWithInstallers(items);
    71         } catch {
    72           finalItems = items;
    73         } finally {
    74           setFiltering(false);
    75         }
    76       }
    77 
    78       if (pageNum === 1) setApps(finalItems);
    79       else setApps((prev) => [...prev, ...finalItems]);
    80       setHasMore(items.length >= 30);
    81     } catch (e: any) {
    82       setError(e.message || '数据加载失败');
    83     } finally {
    84       setLoading(false);
    85       setRefreshing(false);
    86       loadingRef.current = false;
    87     }
    88   }, [activeCategory, onlyInstaller]);
    89 
    90   useFocusEffect(
    91     useCallback(() => {
    92       if (apps.length === 0) loadData(1, false);
    93     }, [apps.length, loadData])
    94   );
    95 
    96   const onCategoryPress = (key: string) => {
    97     setActiveCategory(key);
    98     setPage(1);
    99     setApps([]);

    27 function buildQuery(platform: PlatformType | '全部'): string {
    28   const map: Record<string, string> = {
    29     '全部':    'mobile app stars:>500',
    30     Android:  'android app stars:>1000',
    31     iOS:      'ios app stars:>500',
    32     macOS:    'macos app stars:>500',
    33     Windows:  'windows app stars:>500',
    34     Linux:    'linux app stars:>500',
    35   };
    36   return map[platform] || 'mobile app stars:>500';
    37 }

    17 function useResponsive() {

    19   const isWide = width >= 600;
    20   const contentWidth = isWide ? Math.min(width, 720) : width;
    21   const hPad = isWide ? 24 : 16;

AgentThinkAction(thought='\nThe issue is clear: `filterAppsWithInstallers` is ALWAYS called now (onlyInstaller = true always). This function calls `fetchReleases` for EVERY app fetched (30 apps on home, 15 on discover, 30 on search). \n\nWith anonymous GitHub API: 60 requests/hour total. Loading the home tab alone consumes 30 requests just for filtering. The discover tab consumes another 15. The user would quickly hit the rate limit (403) and see no apps.\n\nBefore, when the toggle was OFF (default), apps loaded fine because `filterAppsWithInstallers` wasn\'t called. Now it\'s always on.\n\nThe fix: Since filterAppsWithInstallers is too expensive for unauthenticated users, we need a smarter approach that doesn\'t consume one API call per app.\n\nOptions:\n1. **Revert to optional filtering** - but user said they want it as default\n2. **Use a different detection strategy** - instead of fetching releases for each app, use topic-based heuristics (if app has topics like \'android-app\', \'ios-app\' etc., assume it has installers)\n3. **Batch smarter** - only filter when a token is configured (not when anonymous)\n4. **Use search query refinement** - add installer-related keywords to the GitHub search query itself to filter out non-installer projects\n\nOption 3 seems most pragmatic: \n- When NO token is configured: don\'t call filterAppsWithInstallers (too expensive, rate limit)\n- When token IS configured: call filterAppsWithInstallers (more API quota available)\n\nBut the user said "过滤功能改为应用的默认功能" - they want it always on. However if it always hits rate limits, no apps load at all.\n\nOption 4 - refine the search query: Add terms like `fork:false` or search for specific topics that indicate installable apps. But GitHub search can\'t filter by "has releases with assets".\n\nActually, the BEST solution is a hybrid approach:\n- Always show apps (don\'t filter via API calls by default)  \n- BUT use a smarter heuristic: check if the app has a `latest_release` or topics suggesting installability\n- OR: filter based on the app\'s topics/language/stars WITHOUT making extra API calls\n\nActually, looking at the data returned from searchRepos → `mapRepoToApp`, we don\'t have release information in the search results. GitHub\'s search API doesn\'t return release assets.\n\nThe real question is: what does the user mean by "加载不出来"? They might be hitting the rate limit due to 30+ extra API calls per page load.\n\nThe fix: Make `filterAppsWithInstallers` conditional on having a token. Without token, skip the filter (show all apps) to avoid rate limiting. With token, filter. This balances UX vs. rate limits.\n\nBut user wants it always on as default... \n\nAlternative: Instead of calling `fetchReleases` for ALL apps, do a "quick check" approach:\n- Only check apps that have installer-suggesting topics (android, ios, windows, etc.)  \n- Or pre-filter by language (Swift, Kotlin, Java, Dart → likely mobile)\n- Or do it in smaller batches with delay\n\nActually the simplest fix that respects user\'s intent while not breaking the app: **Always apply the filter, but handle the 403 rate-limit gracefully by falling back to showing all apps instead of showing nothing.**\n\nLooking at the current code in index.tsx:\n```ts\nif (installerFilter) {\n  setFiltering(true);\n  try {\n    finalItems = await filterAppsWithInstallers(items);\n  } catch {\n    finalItems = items; // fallback to all items on error\n  } finally {\n    setFiltering(false);\n  }\n}\n```\n\nThis DOES fall back to `items` on error! So if rate limit hits, it should still show all items...\n\nBut wait, `filterAppsWithInstallers` uses `Promise.allSettled`, which doesn\'t throw even if individual calls fail. Let me check:\n\n```ts\nexport async function filterAppsWithInstallers(apps: AppItem[]): Promise<AppItem[]> {\n  const results = await Promise.allSettled(\n    apps.map((app) => fetchReleases(app.owner, app.repo, 1))\n  )\n  return apps.filter((_, i) => {\n    const r = results[i]\n    if (r.status !== \'fulfilled\' || r.value.length === 0) return false\n    return r.value.some((release) => hasInstallerAsset(release.assets))\n  })\n}\n```\n\n`Promise.allSettled` never throws - it settles all. If a `fetchReleases` call fails (rejected), the result has `status: \'rejected\'`, and the `filter` returns false for that app. So ALL rejected results are filtered out.\n\nTHIS IS THE BUG! When rate limit is hit (all 30 API calls return 403 → all rejected), `filterAppsWithInstallers` returns an EMPTY array. The catch block in loadData catches NOTHING (filterAppsWithInstallers resolved, not rejected). So `finalItems = []` and the tab shows empty.\n\nThe fix: When ALL releases fetch calls fail (or fail above a threshold), return the original apps array instead of empty array.\n\n```ts\nexport async function filterAppsWithInstallers(apps: AppItem[]): Promise<AppItem[]> {\n  const results = await Promise.allSettled(\n    apps.map((app) => fetchReleases(app.owner, app.repo, 1))\n  )\n  \n  // 如果所有请求都失败（如限流），返回原始列表而不是空数组\n  const failCount = results.filter(r => r.status === \'rejected\').length;\n  if (failCount === results.length) {\n    return apps; // 全部失败时降级展示全部应用\n  }\n  \n  return apps.filter((_, i) => {\n    const r = results[i]\n    if (r.status !== \'fulfilled\' || r.value.length === 0) return false\n    return r.value.some((release) => hasInstallerAsset(release.assets))\n  })\n}\n```\n\nThis is the key fix. But also, we should be smarter: even a partial failure (most fail) should trigger fallback.\n\nActually, let me think about this more. If we have 30 apps and 25 fail (rate limit), we\'d filter based on 5 results. That means we\'d show 0-5 apps max. Still bad UX.\n\nBetter approach: if failure rate > threshold (e.g., > 50%), fall back to showing all apps.\n\nOR: Move `filterAppsWithInstallers` to be rate-limit aware and only run when token is set (sufficient quota).\n\nI\'ll implement:\n1. Fix `filterAppsWithInstallers` to fall back gracefully when most calls fail\n2. Also add a note that this feature works best with a token\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

<action>
**FileEditAction**
Path: [/workspace/app-cblk1rqa5fk1/src/lib/github.ts]
Thought: 两处并行修复：`filterAppsWithInstallers` 限流降级 + 三个 Tab 的 catch 兜底：
Command: str_replace
Old String: ```
/**
 * 批量检查应用是否发布了有效安装包，返回过滤后的列表。
 * 并行拉取每个应用的第一页 releases，仅保留含安装包的应用。
 * 注意：每次调用会消耗 apps.length 个 GitHub API 配额，建议在已配置 Token 的情况下使用。
 */
export async function filterAppsWithInstallers(apps: AppItem[]): Promise<AppItem[]> {
  const results = await Promise.allSettled(
    apps.map((app) => fetchReleases(app.owner, app.repo, 1))
  )
  return apps.filter((_, i) => {
    const r = results[i]
    if (r.status !== 'fulfilled' || r.value.length === 0) return false
    // 只要任意一个 release 含安装包即通过
    return r.value.some((release) => hasInstallerAsset(release.assets))
  })
}
```
New String: ```
/**
 * 批量检查应用是否发布了有效安装包，返回过滤后的列表。
 * 并行拉取每个应用的第一页 releases，仅保留含安装包的应用。
 *
 * 降级策略：若失败率超过 50%（如匿名限流），直接返回原始列表避免全部应用消失。
 */
export async function filterAppsWithInstallers(apps: AppItem[]): Promise<AppItem[]> {
  if (apps.length === 0) return apps

  const results = await Promise.allSettled(
    apps.map((app) => fetchReleases(app.owner, app.repo, 1))
  )

  // 失败率超过 50% → 限流降级，返回原始列表
  const failCount = results.filter((r) => r.status === 'rejected').length
  if (failCount > results.length * 0.5) {
    return apps
  }

  return apps.filter((_, i) => {
    const r = results[i]
    if (r.status !== 'fulfilled' || r.value.length === 0) return false
    // 只要任意一个 release 含安装包即通过
    return r.value.some((release) => hasInstallerAsset(release.assets))
  })
}
```

import { Image } from 'expo-image';
import LetterAvatar from './LetterAvatar';
import { useState } from 'react';

interface AppIconProps {
  url: string | null;
  name: string;
  size?: number;
  className?: string;
}

export default function AppIcon({ url, name, size = 48, className = '' }: AppIconProps) {
  const [error, setError] = useState(false);

  if (!url || error) {
    return <LetterAvatar name={name} size={size} className={className} />;
  }

  return (

New String: ```
/**
 * 应用图标组件 — 级联回退链
 * 按优先级依次尝试以下来源，直到某张图片加载成功：
 *   1. fastlane Android icon（最常见于 Android 开源 App）
 *   2. 仓库根目录 app_icon.png
 *   3. 仓库根目录 icon.png
 *   4. owner.avatar_url（GitHub 用户/组织头像）
 *   5. LetterAvatar（首字母占位）
 */
import { Image } from 'expo-image';
import LetterAvatar from './LetterAvatar';
import { useState, useMemo } from 'react';

interface AppIconProps {
  /** owner GitHub 登录名（用于构建仓库 raw URL） */
  owner?: string;
  /** 仓库名 */
  repo?: string;
  /** owner 头像 URL（最终托底） */
  url: string | null;
  name: string;
  size?: number;
  className?: string;
}

/** 构建按优先级排列的图标 URL 候选列表 */
function buildIconUrls(owner: string | undefined, repo: string | undefined, avatarUrl: string | null): string[] {
  const urls: string[] = [];
  if (owner && repo) {
    const base = `https://raw.githubusercontent.com/${owner}/${repo}/HEAD`;
    // Android Fastlane 图标（512x512，最能代表 App 真实图标）
    urls.push(`${base}/fastlane/metadata/android/en-US/images/icon.png`);
    // iOS Fastlane 图标
    urls.push(`${base}/fastlane/metadata/ios/icon.png`);
    // 常见仓库根目录图标文件名
    urls.push(`${base}/app_icon.png`);
    urls.push(`${base}/icon.png`);
    urls.push(`${base}/logo.png`);
  }
  if (avatarUrl) urls.push(avatarUrl);
  return urls;
}

export default function AppIcon({ owner, repo, url, name, size = 48, className = '' }: AppIconProps) {
  const candidates = useMemo(() => buildIconUrls(owner, repo, url), [owner, repo, url]);
  const [idx, setIdx] = useState(0);

  const currentUrl = candidates[idx] ?? null;

  if (!currentUrl) {
    return <LetterAvatar name={name} size={size} className={className} />;
  }

  return (
    <Image
      className={className}
      source={{ uri: currentUrl }}
      style={{ width: size, height: size, borderRadius: size * 0.24 }}
      contentFit="cover"
      transition={200}
      onError={() => {
        if (idx + 1 < candidates.length) {
          setIdx((i) => i + 1);
        } else {
          // 所有候选均失败，idx 停在末尾触发 LetterAvatar
          setIdx(candidates.length);
        }
      }}
    />
  );
}
```

AgentThinkAction(thought='\nThe issue is that the cascading fallback chain isn\'t finding any real app icons. The `raw.githubusercontent.com` URLs for fastlane metadata and common icon files (app_icon.png, icon.png, logo.png) are all failing for most repos, so they all fall back to LetterAvatar.\n\nThe problem: most GitHub repos don\'t have these specific files. The owner avatar_url IS actually loading but we\'re trying many other URLs first, and they all fail, but the avatar_url should work.\n\nWait - let me re-read the code. After all candidates fail including avatar_url, it shows LetterAvatar. But the user says all are showing letters. So either:\n1. The avatar_url is also failing to load, OR\n2. There\'s a bug in the idx logic\n\nLooking at the code:\n```tsx\nconst candidates = useMemo(() => buildIconUrls(owner, repo, url), [owner, repo, url]);\nconst [idx, setIdx] = useState(0);\nconst currentUrl = candidates[idx] ?? null;\n```\n\nIf `candidates.length` is e.g. 6 (5 raw URLs + 1 avatar), and we keep getting errors:\n- idx=0 fails → setIdx(1)\n- idx=1 fails → setIdx(2)\n- ...\n- idx=4 fails → setIdx(5) - this is avatar_url\n- idx=5 (avatar_url) fails → setIdx(6)\n- idx=6: `candidates[6]` is undefined → `null` → shows LetterAvatar\n\nSo if the avatar_url also fails (network issue, or rate limiting on GitHub avatar CDN), it shows LetterAvatar.\n\nBut wait - previously when just using `avatar_url` directly, it WAS showing the owner avatar. Now after the refactor, it\'s showing all letters. \n\nThe most likely issue: **React\'s useState is not re-initialized when props change**. The `useState(0)` only initializes once. If the component is reused (e.g. in a FlatList), the `idx` state might carry over from a previous render, causing `candidates[idx]` to be out of bounds or wrong.\n\nActually wait - FlatList reuses components via key. If the key changes, the component remounts. But if the key stays the same and props (owner/repo) change, then `idx` stays at whatever it was before (possibly pointing to index 6 = undefined = null = LetterAvatar).\n\nAlso another issue: `useMemo` recalculates `candidates` when `owner/repo/url` change, but `idx` state does NOT reset. So if `candidates` becomes a new array with 6 items but `idx` is already 6 from the previous render, we immediately show LetterAvatar.\n\nThe fix: use a `key` based on `${owner}/${repo}` to reset the component, OR use `useEffect` to reset `idx` when `owner/repo/url` change.\n\nBetter fix: reset `idx` to 0 when the candidates change:\n```tsx\nconst [idx, setIdx] = useState(0);\nconst prevCandidatesRef = useRef(candidates);\nif (prevCandidatesRef.current !== candidates) {\n  prevCandidatesRef.current = candidates;\n  setIdx(0); // reset when candidates change\n}\n```\n\nOr more cleanly, use a `key` prop from the parent based on `${owner}/${repo}`. This means for each app card, we\'re firing 5 failed requests before getting to the avatar. This is a lot of unnecessary network traffic and causes visible delay.\n\nA smarter approach: Instead of trying all these raw URLs blindly, I should be more selective. Use the owner\'s avatar (what we had before) - not ideal but works\n2. Use `https://avatars.githubusercontent.com/{owner}` which is the same as owner avatar\n3. Use the GitHub repo\'s social preview: `https://opengraph.githubassets.com/1/{owner}/{repo}` - this is the card image, not ideal\n4. Thought: 问题根因：`useState(0)` 在组件复用时不会重置，当候选列表（`candidates`）因 `owner/repo` 变化重新生成后，旧的 `idx` 仍指向越界位置，直接跳到 `LetterAvatar`。同时候选 URL 过多（5 个 404），网络噪声大。修复方案：派生状态同步重置 `idx` + 精简候选列表：

/**
 * 应用图标组件 — 级联回退链
 * 按优先级依次尝试以下来源，直到某张图片加载成功：
 *   1. fastlane Android icon（最常见于 Android 开源 App）
 *   2. 仓库根目录 app_icon.png
 *   3. 仓库根目录 icon.png
 *   4. owner.avatar_url（GitHub 用户/组织头像）
 *   5. LetterAvatar（首字母占位）
 */
import { Image } from 'expo-image';
import LetterAvatar from './LetterAvatar';
import { useState, useMemo } from 'react';

interface AppIconProps {
  /** owner GitHub 登录名（用于构建仓库 raw URL） */
  owner?: string;
  /** 仓库名 */
  repo?: string;
  /** owner 头像 URL（最终托底） */
  url: string | null;
  name: string;
  size?: number;
  className?: string;
}

/** 构建按优先级排列的图标 URL 候选列表 */
function buildIconUrls(owner: string | undefined, repo: string | undefined, avatarUrl: string | null): string[] {
  const urls: string[] = [];
  if (owner && repo) {
    const base = `https://raw.githubusercontent.com/${owner}/${repo}/HEAD`;
    // Android Fastlane 图标（512x512，最能代表 App 真实图标）
    urls.push(`${base}/fastlane/metadata/android/en-US/images/icon.png`);
    // iOS Fastlane 图标
    urls.push(`${base}/fastlane/metadata/ios/icon.png`);
    // 常见仓库根目录图标文件名
    urls.push(`${base}/app_icon.png`);
    urls.push(`${base}/icon.png`);
    urls.push(`${base}/logo.png`);
  }
  if (avatarUrl) urls.push(avatarUrl);
  return urls;
}

export default function AppIcon({ owner, repo, url, name, size = 48, className = '' }: AppIconProps) {
  const candidates = useMemo(() => buildIconUrls(owner, repo, url), [owner, repo, url]);
  const [idx, setIdx] = useState(0);

  const currentUrl = candidates[idx] ?? null;

  if (!currentUrl) {
    return <LetterAvatar name={name} size={size} className={className} />;
  }

  return (
    <Image
      className={className}
      source={{ uri: currentUrl }}
      style={{ width: size, height: size, borderRadius: size * 0.24 }}
      contentFit="cover"
      transition={200}
      onError={() => {
        if (idx + 1 < candidates.length) {
          setIdx((i) => i + 1);
        } else {
          // 所有候选均失败，idx 停在末尾触发 LetterAvatar
          setIdx(candidates.length);
        }
      }}
    />
  );
}
```
New String: ```
/**
 * 应用图标组件 — 级联回退链
 * 按优先级依次尝试以下来源，直到某张图片加载成功：
 *   1. fastlane Android icon（常见于 Android 开源 App）
 *   2. 仓库根目录 icon.png
 *   3. owner.avatar_url（GitHub 用户/组织头像，最可靠的托底）
 *   4. LetterAvatar（首字母占位，网络完全不可用时兜底）
 *
 * 关键设计：candidates 引用变化时同步重置 failCount（派生状态），
 * 避免 FlatList 组件复用时 failCount 保留旧值导致直接跳到 LetterAvatar。
 */
import { Image } from 'expo-image';
import LetterAvatar from './LetterAvatar';
import { useState, useMemo, useRef } from 'react';

interface AppIconProps {
  /** owner GitHub 登录名（用于构建仓库 raw URL） */
  owner?: string;
  /** 仓库名 */
  repo?: string;
  /** owner 头像 URL（最终托底） */
  url: string | null;
  name: string;
  size?: number;
  className?: string;
}

/** 构建按优先级排列的图标 URL 候选列表（精简为 3 项以减少无效请求） */
function buildIconUrls(owner: string | undefined, repo: string | undefined, avatarUrl: string | null): string[] {
  const urls: string[] = [];
  if (owner && repo) {
    const base = `https://raw.githubusercontent.com/${owner}/${repo}/HEAD`;
    // Android Fastlane 图标（512×512，最能代表 App 真实图标）
    urls.push(`${base}/fastlane/metadata/android/en-US/images/icon.png`);
    // 常见仓库根目录图标
    urls.push(`${base}/icon.png`);
  }
  // owner 头像：最可靠的兜底，几乎所有 GitHub 仓库都有
  if (avatarUrl) urls.push(avatarUrl);
  return urls;
}

export default function AppIcon({ owner, repo, url, name, size = 48, className = '' }: AppIconProps) {
  const candidates = useMemo(() => buildIconUrls(owner, repo, url), [owner, repo, url]);

  // 用 ref 追踪上一次 candidates 引用，派生状态同步重置 failCount
  const prevCandidatesRef = useRef(candidates);
  const [failCount, setFailCount] = useState(0);

  // 在渲染阶段同步重置（等价于 getDerivedStateFromProps），React 会立即以新 state 重新渲染
  if (prevCandidatesRef.current !== candidates) {
    prevCandidatesRef.current = candidates;
    // 直接 setState 会在本次 render 后同步刷新，符合 React 文档规范
    setFailCount(0);
  }

  const currentUrl = candidates[failCount] ?? null;

  if (!currentUrl) {
    return <LetterAvatar name={name} size={size} className={className} />;
  }

  return (
    <Image
      source={{ uri: currentUrl }}
      style={{ width: size, height: size, borderRadius: size * 0.24 }}
      contentFit="cover"
      transition={200}
      onError={() =>
        setFailCount((c) => c + 1)
      }
    />
  );
}
```

  name: string;
  size?: number;
  className?: string;
}

/** 构建按优先级排列的图标 URL 候选列表（精简为 3 项以减少无效请求） */
function buildIconUrls(owner: string | undefined, repo: string | undefined, avatarUrl: string | null): string[] {
  const urls: string[] = [];
  if (owner && repo) {
    const base = `https://raw.githubusercontent.com/${owner}/${repo}/HEAD`;
    // Android Fastlane 图标（512×512，最能代表 App 真实图标）
    urls.push(`${base}/fastlane/metadata/android/en-US/images/icon.png`);
    // 常见仓库根目录图标
    urls.push(`${base}/icon.png`);
  }
  // owner 头像：最可靠的兜底，几乎所有 GitHub 仓库都有
  if (avatarUrl) urls.push(avatarUrl);
  return urls;
}

export default function AppIcon({ owner, repo, url, name, size = 48, className = '' }: AppIconProps) {
  const candidates = useMemo(() => buildIconUrls(owner, repo, url), [owner, repo, url]);

  // 用 ref 追踪上一次 candidates 引用，派生状态同步重置 failCount
  const prevCandidatesRef = useRef(candidates);
  const [failCount, setFailCount] = useState(0);

  // 在渲染阶段同步重置（等价于 getDerivedStateFromProps），React 会立即以新 state 重新渲染
  if (prevCandidatesRef.current !== candidates) {
    prevCandidatesRef.current = candidates;
    // 直接 setState 会在本次 render 后同步刷新，符合 React 文档规范
    setFailCount(0);
  }

  const currentUrl = candidates[failCount] ?? null;

  if (!currentUrl) {
    return <LetterAvatar name={name} size={size} className={className} />;
  }

  return (
    <Image
      source={{ uri: currentUrl }}
      style={{ width: size, height: size, borderRadius: size * 0.24 }}
      contentFit="cover"
      transition={200}
      onError={() =>
        setFailCount((c) => c + 1)
      }
    />
  );
}
```
New String: ```
/**
 * 应用图标组件 — 级联回退链
 * 按优先级依次尝试：fastlane Android icon → 根目录 icon.png → owner 头像 → LetterAvatar
 *
 * 状态管理：将候选列表标识 (iconKey) 与失败计数 (failCount) 存入同一个 state 对象。
 * 当 iconKey 变化时（FlatList 复用组件、切换应用）在渲染阶段同步派生重置 failCount，
 * 避免 useRef 方案在 StrictMode 双调用下失效的问题。
 */
import { Image } from 'expo-image';
import LetterAvatar from './LetterAvatar';
import { useState, useMemo } from 'react';

interface AppIconProps {
  owner?: string;
  repo?: string;
  url: string | null;
  name: string;
  size?: number;
  className?: string;
}

function buildIconUrls(owner: string | undefined, repo: string | undefined, avatarUrl: string | null): string[] {
  const urls: string[] = [];
  if (owner && repo) {
    const base = `https://raw.githubusercontent.com/${owner}/${repo}/HEAD`;
    urls.push(`${base}/fastlane/metadata/android/en-US/images/icon.png`);
    urls.push(`${base}/icon.png`);
  }
  if (avatarUrl) urls.push(avatarUrl);
  return urls;
}

export default function AppIcon({ owner, repo, url, name, size = 48, className = '' }: AppIconProps) {
  const candidates = useMemo(() => buildIconUrls(owner, repo, url), [owner, repo, url]);
  // 用 join 生成稳定字符串 key，标识当前候选列表身份
  const iconKey = candidates.join('||');

  // state 同时持有 key + failCount，当 key 变化时在渲染阶段派生重置（getDerivedStateFromProps 模式）
  const [iconState, setIconState] = useState({ key: iconKey, failCount: 0 });

  // 若 key 已变化，立即派生出新 state（下一 tick 生效），本次渲染用 effectiveCount=0
  let effectiveCount = iconState.failCount;
  if (iconState.key !== iconKey) {
    effectiveCount = 0;
    // 在渲染中调用 setState：React 会丢弃本次渲染结果并以新 state 重新渲染（官方推荐模式）
    setIconState({ key: iconKey, failCount: 0 });
  }

  const currentUrl = candidates[effectiveCount] ?? null;

  if (!currentUrl) {
    return <LetterAvatar name={name} size={size} className={className} />;
  }

  return (
    <Image
      source={{ uri: currentUrl }}
      style={{ width: size, height: size, borderRadius: size * 0.24 }}
      contentFit="cover"
      transition={200}
      onError={() =>
        setIconState((prev) =>
          // 只在 key 未变化时递增，防止并发更新污染新 key 的状态
          prev.key === iconKey
            ? { key: prev.key, failCount: prev.failCount + 1 }
            : prev
        )
      }
    />
  );
}
```

New String: ```
/**
 * 应用图标组件
 *
 * GitHub API 不提供仓库的真实应用图标，仅有 owner.avatar_url（所有者/组织头像）。
 * 本组件直接展示 avatar_url，加载失败时降级为首字母占位（LetterAvatar）。
 *
 * 注意：raw.githubusercontent.com 上的 fastlane/icon.png 仅极少数仓库存在，
 * 批量探测会产生大量 404 请求，并在部分环境中导致 onError 回调异常，
 * 造成所有图标都显示字母，因此不再使用级联回退方案。
 */
import { Image } from 'expo-image';
import LetterAvatar from './LetterAvatar';
import { useState } from 'react';

interface AppIconProps {
  owner?: string;
  repo?: string;
  url: string | null;
  name: string;
  size?: number;
  className?: string;
}

export default function AppIcon({ url, name, size = 48, className = '' }: AppIconProps) {
  const [error, setError] = useState(false);

  if (!url || error) {
    return <LetterAvatar name={name} size={size} className={className} />;
  }

  return (
    <Image
      source={{ uri: url }}
      style={{ width: size, height: size, borderRadius: size * 0.24 }}
      contentFit="cover"
      transition={200}
      onError={() => setError(true)}
    />
  );
}

     1 /**
     2  * 应用图标组件
     3  *
     4  * GitHub API 不提供仓库的真实应用图标，仅有 owner.avatar_url（所有者/组织头像）。
     5  * 本组件直接展示 avatar_url，加载失败时降级为首字母占位（LetterAvatar）。
     6  *
     7  * 注意：raw.githubusercontent.com 上的 fastlane/icon.png 仅极少数仓库存在，
     8  * 批量探测会产生大量 404 请求，并在部分环境中导致 onError 回调异常，
     9  * 造成所有图标都显示字母，因此不再使用级联回退方案。
    10  */
    11 import { Image } from 'expo-image';
    12 import LetterAvatar from './LetterAvatar';
    13 import { useState } from 'react';
    14 
    15 interface AppIconProps {
    16   owner?: string;
    17   repo?: string;
    18   url: string | null;
    19   name: string;
    20   size?: number;
    21   className?: string;
    22 }
    23 
    24 export default function AppIcon({ url, name, size = 48, className = '' }: AppIconProps) {
    25   const [error, setError] = useState(false);
    26 
    27   if (!url || error) {
    28     return <LetterAvatar name={name} size={size} className={className} />;
    29   }
    30 
    31   return (
    32     <Image
    33       source={{ uri: url }}
    34       style={{ width: size, height: size, borderRadius: size * 0.24 }}
    35       contentFit="cover"
    36       transition={200}
    37       onError={() => setError(true)}
    38     />
    39   );
    40 }
    41

<action>
**FileEditAction**
Path: [/workspace/app-cblk1rqa5fk1/src/components/openappstore/AppIcon.tsx]
Thought: 原因很清楚：`contentFit="cover"` 会裁剪图片填满容器（类似 CSS `object-fit: cover`）。GitHub 头像是正方形，而应用圆角卡片也是正方形，两者等比，正常情况不应裁剪。但如果图片本身不是正方形（比如横版 banner 图），`cover` 就会裁剪放大。

修复：改为 `contentFit="contain"` 完整显示图片，并加白色背景防止透明区域：
Command: str_replace
Old String: ```
  return (
    <Image
      source={{ uri: url }}
      style={{ width: size, height: size, borderRadius: size * 0.24 }}
      contentFit="cover"
      transition={200}
      onError={() => setError(true)}
    />
  );
```
New String: ```
  return (
    <Image
      source={{ uri: url }}
      style={{ width: size, height: size, borderRadius: size * 0.24, backgroundColor: '#F5F5F5' }}
      contentFit="contain"
      transition={200}
      onError={() => setError(true)}
    />
  );
```

</action>

The GitHub avatar_url URLs typically look like:\n`https://avatars.githubusercontent.com/u/12345?v=4`\n\nThese are square images (usually 460x460 or similar), so `contain` should work fine.\n\nBut wait - the `url` that\'s being used is `app.avatar_url` which comes from `item.owner?.avatar_url`. GitHub avatar URLs by default serve a small image. When requested without size parameter, they might redirect. But that shouldn\'t cause clipping.\n\nActually, I wonder if the issue is with `expo-image`\'s `contentFit="contain"` behavior. Let me think about this more carefully.\n\nIn `expo-image`, `contentFit="contain"` should work like CSS `object-fit: contain` - it scales the image to fit within the container while maintaining aspect ratio, and doesn\'t crop. This should be correct.\n\nBut wait - could the issue be with `borderRadius` causing visual clipping? With `borderRadius: size * 0.24` and no `overflow: \'hidden\'`, the rounded corners are applied to the view but the image might still render outside those bounds on some platforms.\n\nActually, for `expo-image`, the `borderRadius` in `style` should be applied directly to the image component and it handles the clipping internally. So that should be fine.\n\nLet me think about what else could cause this...\n\nOne possible issue: the GitHub avatar URL might be returning a larger image that gets scaled down, but `contentFit="contain"` should handle that.\n\nAnother thought: maybe the issue is that `expo-image` on certain platforms doesn\'t respect `contentFit="contain"` correctly. \n\nActually, wait. The image source itself is larger than the container (e.g., GitHub serves a high-res avatar) and it\'s being scaled to fill\n2. The `borderRadius` is clipping the corners visually in a way that makes it look wrong\n\nBut `contentFit="contain"` should prevent scaling beyond the container size...\n\nActually, I just realized something important. On web, `expo-image` renders as an `img` tag, and `borderRadius` + `contentFit` might not clip properly without a wrapper `View` with `overflow: \'hidden\'`.\n\nAlso, GitHub avatar URLs by default return 460x460 images. When displayed in a 56x56 container with `contain`, they should be scaled down - but perhaps the `borderRadius` is causing visual issues.\n\nThe most robust fix:\n1. Wrap in a `View` with `overflow: \'hidden\'` and `borderRadius` applied to the wrapper\n2. Use `style={{ width: size, height: size }}` on the Image (no borderRadius on Image itself)\n3. The background color goes on the wrapper View\n4. Optionally normalize GitHub avatar URLs to request square images at the right size\n\nThis is the standard pattern in React Native for rounded images - the `borderRadius` + `overflow: \'hidden\'` on a wrapper View provides reliable clipping on all platforms.\n\nThe key insight: `expo-image` with `borderRadius` in `style` might not clip the image content itself (just the container box), while `View` with `overflow: \'hidden\'` + `borderRadius` creates a proper clip mask.\n\nLet me implement the wrapper approach.\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

<action>
**FileEditAction**
Path: [/workspace/app-cblk1rqa5fk1/src/components/openappstore/AppIcon.tsx]
Thought: 根本原因：直接在 `expo-image` 的 `style` 上设置 `borderRadius` 在部分平台上只裁剪容器边框，不裁剪图片内容本身。标准解法是用 `View` 包裹并在 View 上设置 `borderRadius + overflow: 'hidden'`，这样图片内容才会被正确裁剪到圆角区域内。
Command: str_replace
Old String: ```
/**
 * 应用图标组件
 *
 * GitHub API 不提供仓库的真实应用图标，仅有 owner.avatar_url（所有者/组织头像）。
 * 本组件直接展示 avatar_url，加载失败时降级为首字母占位（LetterAvatar）。
 *
 * 注意：raw.githubusercontent.com 上的 fastlane/icon.png 仅极少数仓库存在，
 * 批量探测会产生大量 404 请求，并在部分环境中导致 onError 回调异常，
 * 造成所有图标都显示字母，因此不再使用级联回退方案。
 */
import { Image } from 'expo-image';
import LetterAvatar from './LetterAvatar';
import { useState } from 'react';

interface AppIconProps {
  owner?: string;
  repo?: string;
  url: string | null;
  name: string;
  size?: number;
  className?: string;
}

export default function AppIcon({ url, name, size = 48, className = '' }: AppIconProps) {
  const [error, setError] = useState(false);

  if (!url || error) {
    return <LetterAvatar name={name} size={size} className={className} />;
  }

  return (
    <Image
      source={{ uri: url }}
      style={{ width: size, height: size, borderRadius: size * 0.24, backgroundColor: '#F5F5F5' }}
      contentFit="contain"
      transition={200}
      onError={() => setError(true)}
    />
  );
}
```
New String: ```
/**
 * 应用图标组件
 *
 * GitHub API 不提供仓库的真实应用图标，仅有 owner.avatar_url（所有者/组织头像）。
 * 本组件直接展示 avatar_url，加载失败时降级为首字母占位（LetterAvatar）。
 *
 * 渲染方案：用 View 包裹 Image 并在 View 上设置 borderRadius + overflow:'hidden'。
 * 直接在 expo-image style 上设置 borderRadius 在部分平台只裁剪容器边框，
 * 不裁剪图片内容，导致图片溢出；wrapper View 方案可跨平台可靠裁剪。
 */
import { View } from 'react-native';
import { Image } from 'expo-image';
import LetterAvatar from './LetterAvatar';
import { useState } from 'react';

interface AppIconProps {
  owner?: string;
  repo?: string;
  url: string | null;
  name: string;
  size?: number;
  className?: string;
}

export default function AppIcon({ url, name, size = 48, className = '' }: AppIconProps) {
  const [error, setError] = useState(false);

  if (!url || error) {
    return <LetterAvatar name={name} size={size} className={className} />;
  }

  return (
    <View
      style={{
        width: size,
        height: size,
        borderRadius: size * 0.24,
        overflow: 'hidden',
        backgroundColor: '#F5F5F5',
      }}
    >
      <Image
        source={{ uri: url }}
        style={{ width: size, height: size }}
        contentFit="contain"
        transition={200}
        onError={() => setError(true)}
      />
    </View>
  );
}
```

</action>

     1 /**
     2  * 应用图标组件

     4  * GitHub API 不提供仓库的真实应用图标，仅有 owner.avatar_url（所有者/组织头像）。
     5  * 本组件直接展示 avatar_url，加载失败时降级为首字母占位（LetterAvatar）。
     6  *
     7  * 渲染方案：用 View 包裹 Image 并在 View 上设置 borderRadius + overflow:'hidden'。

     9  * 不裁剪图片内容，导致图片溢出；wrapper View 方案可跨平台可靠裁剪。
    10  */
    11 import { View } from 'react-native';
    12 import { Image } from 'expo-image';
    13 import LetterAvatar from './LetterAvatar';
    14 import { useState } from 'react';
    15 
    16 interface AppIconProps {
    17   owner?: string;
    18   repo?: string;
    19   url: string | null;
    20   name: string;
    21   size?: number;
    22   className?: string;
    23 }
    24 
    25 export default function AppIcon({ url, name, size = 48, className = '' }: AppIconProps) {
    26   const [error, setError] = useState(false);
    27 
    28   if (!url || error) {
    29     return <LetterAvatar name={name} size={size} className={className} />;
    30   }
    31 
    32   return (
    33     <View
    34       style={{
    35         width: size,
    36         height: size,
    37         borderRadius: size * 0.24,
    38         overflow: 'hidden',
    39         backgroundColor: '#F5F5F5',
    40       }}
    41     >
    42       <Image
    43         source={{ uri: url }}
    44         style={{ width: size, height: size }}
    45         contentFit="contain"
    46         transition={200}
    47         onError={() => setError(true)}
    48       />
    49     </View>
    50   );
    51 }

AgentThinkAction(thought='\nThe user is asking about why the APP icon (the launcher icon on the device home screen) is being clipped and enlarged. This is different from the `AppIcon` component (which shows GitHub owner avatars in the app UI).\n\nThe user is likely referring to the Android **adaptive icon** system. Here\'s the issue:\n\n**Android Adaptive Icon clipping:**\nIn `app.json`, the Android config uses:\n```json\n"adaptiveIcon": {\n  "foregroundImage": "./assets/adaptive-icon.png",\n  "backgroundColor": "#FFFFFF"\n}\n```\n\nAndroid adaptive icons crop the foreground image. The Android adaptive icon spec requires that the actual icon content (safe zone) must be within the **central 66px out of 108px** (or about 66.7% of the total size). The outer ring is masked/cropped by the launcher.\n\nOur SVG was 192×192 and we converted it to 1024×1024 PNG filling the entire canvas. When used as an adaptive icon foreground, Android crops it to a circle/squircle/rounded square, cutting off the edges.\n\nFor adaptive icons, the safe zone is the **central 72dp of the 108dp icon** (66.7%). So if the icon image is 1024×1024, the safe zone is approximately 1024 × (72/108) ≈ 683×683 pixels centered.\n\nThe fix: \n1. For the `adaptiveIcon.foregroundImage`, the actual icon art should be placed in the central ~66% of the image, with transparent/empty padding around it\n2. OR: use the same `icon.png` for both `icon` and replace `foregroundImage` with it, but set `backgroundColor` to match the icon background\n\nActually the better approach for this specific case:\n- The SVG has a white background (#FCFDFC)  \n- We can either:\n  a. Add padding to the adaptive icon (resize the icon to 66% within 1024×1024 with padding)\n  b. Remove the adaptive icon config and just use the regular icon for Android too\n\nThe safest fix is to create a properly padded adaptive icon. The icon content should be ~66% of the total size, centered.\n\nLet me recalculate: \n- Output PNG: 1024×1024\n- Safe zone (content area): 66% × 1024 = ~677px\n- Padding on each side: (1024 - 677) / 2 = ~173px\n\nSo we need to:\n1. Create adaptive-icon.png: 1024×1024 with the actual icon art scaled to 677×677 centered, with 173px padding on each side\n\nOR even simpler: \n- Set `foregroundImage` padding: just make the image smaller within the canvas\n- This means the icon will appear smaller on Android but won\'t be clipped\n\nActually the simplest fix is to recreate the adaptive-icon.png with proper padding. The content should fill only ~72% of the image (to account for the masking).\n\nLet me use Python/cairosvg to:\n1. Convert SVG to 677×677 \n2. Paste it centered on a 1024×1024 transparent canvas\n\nFor `icon.png` (iOS and general), the full 1024×1024 is fine because iOS applies its own mask.\n\nWait, but the user said "APP的图标会被裁剪放大" - they might be saying this in the web preview or the app itself (maybe they see the app icon inside the app store list, not the launcher icon)?\n\nActually re-reading: "APP的图标" likely refers to the launcher icon shown when the app is installed on a device, not the in-app AppIcon component. The Android adaptive icon is getting clipped.\n\nLet me fix the adaptive-icon.png to add proper safe-zone padding.\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

<action>
**CmdRunAction (source=EventSource.AGENT, is_input=False)**
THOUGHT: 问题根因已确定：**Android Adaptive Icon 安全区规范**。

Android 自适应图标要求前景图(`foregroundImage`)的实际内容只能占整张图片尺寸的约 **66%**（108dp 中只有 72dp 是安全区），外围 17% 会被系统用圆形/方形遮罩裁掉。我们当前的 `adaptive-icon.png` 图标内容填满了整个 1024×1024 画布，所以边缘被裁掉后视觉上看起来"放大变形"了。

修复：重新生成 `adaptive-icon.png`，将图标内容缩小到画布的 66%，四周留透明安全边距：
COMMAND:
python3 - <<'EOF'
from PIL import Image
import io, cairosvg

svg_path = "/workspace/app-cblk1rqa5fk1/tasks/md_20260614_213612_2.txt"
with open(svg_path, "rb") as f:
    svg_data = f.read()

CANVAS = 1024          # adaptive-icon 画布总尺寸
SAFE_RATIO = 0.66      # Android 安全区比例（72/108）
CONTENT = int(CANVAS * SAFE_RATIO)   # 676px — 实际内容区
PADDING = (CANVAS - CONTENT) // 2    # 每侧留 174px 边距

# 1. icon.png — 完整 1024×1024（iOS/通用，iOS 自己处理遮罩）
png_full = cairosvg.svg2png(bytestring=svg_data, output_width=CANVAS, output_height=CANVAS)
with open("/workspace/app-cblk1rqa5fk1/assets/icon.png", "wb") as f:
    f.write(png_full)

# 2. adaptive-icon.png — 内容缩至 66%，四周填充透明边距
png_content = cairosvg.svg2png(bytestring=svg_data, output_width=CONTENT, output_height=CONTENT)
content_img = Image.open(io.BytesIO(png_content)).convert("RGBA")

canvas = Image.new("RGBA", (CANVAS, CANVAS), (0, 0, 0, 0))  # 透明底
canvas.paste(content_img, (PADDING, PADDING))

canvas.save("/workspace/app-cblk1rqa5fk1/assets/adaptive-icon.png", "PNG")

# 验证
final = Image.open("/workspace/app-cblk1rqa5fk1/assets/adaptive-icon.png")
print(f"adaptive-icon: {final.size}, mode={final.mode}")
print(f"内容区={CONTENT}px，每侧边距={PADDING}px，安全比例={CONTENT/CANVAS:.2%}")
EOF
</action>

    27     } catch {

    32   } else {
    33     _safDirUri = null;
    34   }
    35   return null;
    36 }
